\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// GET /notifications \u2014 Get notifications for instructor from D1\ninstructorRoutes.get('/notifications', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    let instructorId: string;\n\n    if (authRole === 'admin') {\n      instructorId = c.req.query('instructorId') || '';\n      if (!instructorId) {\n        return c.json({ error: 'instructorId query param required for admin access' }, 400);\n      }\n    } else {\n      instructorId = c.get('instructorId');\n    }\n\n    const limit = parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '20');\n    const offset = parseInt(c.req.query('offset') || '0');\n    const unreadOnly = c.req.query('unread') === 'true';\n\n    let query = 'SELECT * FROM notifications WHERE user_id = ?';\n    const params: unknown[] = [instructorId];\n\n    if (unreadOnly) {\n      query += ' AND read = 0';\n    }\n\n    query += ' ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?';\n    params.push(limit, offset);\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(query).bind(...params).all();\n\n    // Get total count\n    let countQuery = 'SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM notifications WHERE user_id = ?';\n    const countParams: unknown[] = [instructorId];\n    if (unreadOnly) {\n      countQuery += ' AND read = 0';\n    }\n    const countResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(countQuery).bind(...countParams).first<{ total: number }>();\n    const total = countResult?.total || 0;\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, notifications: result.results, total });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// PUT /notifications/:id/read \u2014 Mark notification as read in D1\ninstructorRoutes.put('/notifications/:id/read', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const notificationId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'UPDATE notifications SET read = 1 WHERE id = ?'\n    ).bind(notificationId).run();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, message: 'Notification marked as read' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// PUT /notifications/read-all \u2014 Mark all notifications as read\ninstructorRoutes.put('/notifications/read-all', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    let instructorId: string;\n\n    if (authRole === 'admin') {\n      instructorId = c.req.query('instructorId') || '';\n      if (!instructorId) {\n        return c.json({ error: 'instructorId query param required for admin access' }, 400);\n      }\n    } else {\n      instructorId = c.get('instructorId');\n    }\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'UPDATE notifications SET read = 1 WHERE user_id = ? AND read = 0'\n    ).bind(instructorId).run();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, message: 'All notifications marked as read' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// SUPPORT TICKET ROUTES (instructorOrAdmin)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// POST /support/tickets \u2014 Create support ticket\ninstructorRoutes.post('/support/tickets', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    let instructorId: string;\n    let instructorEmail: string;\n    let instructorName: string;\n\n    if (authRole === 'admin') {\n      instructorId = c.req.query('instructorId') || '';\n      instructorEmail = c.req.query('instructorEmail') || '';\n      instructorName = c.req.query('instructorName') || '';\n    } else {\n      instructorId = c.get('instructorId');\n      instructorEmail = c.get('instructorEmail');\n      instructorName = c.get('instructorName');\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { category, subject, description, priority } = body;\n\n    if (!category || !subject || !description) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'category, subject, and description are required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const ticketId = `TK-${String(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000))}`;\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO support_tickets (ticket_id, user_id, name, email, category, subject, description, priority, status, created_at, updated_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'open', ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      ticketId,\n      instructorId,\n      instructorName,\n      instructorEmail,\n      category,\n      subject,\n      description,\n      priority || 'medium',\n      now,\n      now\n    ).run();\n\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      ticket: {\n        ticketId,\n        status: 'open',\n        createdAt: now,\n      },\n    }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /support/tickets \u2014 List instructor's tickets\ninstructorRoutes.get('/support/tickets', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    let instructorId: string;\n\n    if (authRole === 'admin') {\n      instructorId = c.req.query('instructorId') || '';\n      if (!instructorId) {\n        return c.json({ error: 'instructorId query param required for admin access' }, 400);\n      }\n    } else {\n      instructorId = c.get('instructorId');\n    }\n\n    const limit = parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '20');\n    const offset = parseInt(c.req.query('offset') || '0');\n    const status = c.req.query('status');\n\n    let query = 'SELECT * FROM support_tickets WHERE user_id = ?';\n    const params: unknown[] = [instructorId];\n\n    if (status) {\n      query += ' AND status = ?';\n      params.push(status);\n    }\n\n    query += ' ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?';\n    params.push(limit, offset);\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(query).bind(...params).all();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, tickets: result.results });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// DASHBOARD ROUTE (instructorOrAdmin)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// GET /dashboard \u2014 Dashboard stats\ninstructorRoutes.get('/dashboard', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    let instructorId: string;\n\n    if (authRole === 'admin') {\n      instructorId = c.req.query('instructorId') || '';\n      if (!instructorId) {\n        return c.json({ error: 'instructorId query param required for admin access' }, 400);\n      }\n    } else {\n      instructorId = c.get('instructorId');\n    }\n\n    // Get course count from D1 courses table\n    let courseCount = 0;\n    try {\n      const courseCountResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM courses WHERE instructor_id = ?'\n      ).bind(instructorId).first<{ total: number }>();\n      courseCount = courseCountResult?.total || 0;\n    } catch {}\n\n    // Also count from course_instructors\n    let subjectCourseCount = 0;\n    try {\n      const subjectResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT course_id) as count FROM course_instructors WHERE instructor_id = ?'\n      ).bind(instructorId).first<{ count: number }>();\n      subjectCourseCount = subjectResult?.count || 0;\n    } catch {}\n    courseCount = Math.max(courseCount, subjectCourseCount);\n\n    // Total students across all courses \u2014 get all course IDs for this instructor\n    let totalStudents = 0;\n    try {\n      // Get enrollment count for courses where instructor_id matches in courses table\n      const studentCountResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.user_id) as total\n        FROM enrollments e\n        INNER JOIN courses c ON e.course_id = c.id\n        WHERE c.instructor_id = ?\n      `).bind(instructorId).first<{ total: number }>();\n      totalStudents = studentCountResult?.total || 0;\n\n      // Also add students from course_instructors assigned courses\n      const subjectStudentResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT e.user_id) as total\n        FROM enrollments e\n        INNER JOIN course_instructors ci ON e.course_id = ci.course_id\n        WHERE ci.instructor_id = ?\n      `).bind(instructorId).first<{ total: number }>();\n      totalStudents = Math.max(totalStudents, subjectStudentResult?.total || 0);\n    } catch {}\n\n    // Upcoming live classes\n    let upcomingClasses = 0;\n    try {\n      const classResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        \"SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM live_class_schedules WHERE instructor_id = ? AND scheduled_at > datetime('now') AND is_active = 1\"\n      ).bind(instructorId).first<{ count: number }>();\n      upcomingClasses = classResult?.count || 0;\n    } catch {}\n\n    // Review stats\n    let avgRating = 0;\n    let totalReviews = 0;\n    try {\n      const ratingStats = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT AVG(rating) as avg, COUNT(*) as count FROM instructor_reviews WHERE instructor_id = ?'\n      ).bind(instructorId).first<{ avg: number; count: number }>();\n      avgRating = ratingStats?.avg ? Math.round(ratingStats.avg * 10) / 10 : 0;\n      totalReviews = ratingStats?.count || 0;\n    } catch {}\n\n    // Revenue \u2014 get all course IDs for this instructor and sum payments\n    let totalRevenue = 0;\n    try {\n      // Revenue from courses where instructor_id matches directly\n      const directRevenue = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(p.amount), 0) as total\n        FROM payments p\n        INNER JOIN courses c ON p.course_id = c.id\n        WHERE c.instructor_id = ? AND p.status = 'completed'\n      `).bind(instructorId).first<{ total: number }>();\n      totalRevenue = directRevenue?.total || 0;\n\n      // Also add revenue from course_subjects assigned courses\n      const subjectRevenue = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        SELECT COALESCE(SUM(p.amount), 0) as total\n        FROM payments p\n        INNER JOIN course_subjects cs ON p.course_id = cs.course_id\n        WHERE cs.instructor_id = ? AND p.status = 'completed'\n      `).bind(instructorId).first<{ total: number }>();\n      totalRevenue = Math.max(totalRevenue, subjectRevenue?.total || 0);\n    } catch {}\n\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      dashboard: {\n        courseCount,\n        totalStudents,\n        upcomingClasses,\n        avgRating,\n        totalReviews,\n        totalRevenue,\n      },\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// COURSE CRUD (Create, Update \u2014 instructors can only manage their own courses)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// POST /courses \u2014 Create a new course (instructor is auto-assigned)\ninstructorRoutes.post('/courses', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { title, description, slug, technology_id, semester, level, price_bdt, is_published, thumbnail_url } = body;\n\n    if (!title) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'title is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const courseId = generateId();\n    const courseSlug = slug || slugify(title);\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO courses (id, title, slug, description, technology_id, semester, level, price_bdt, is_published, instructor_id, thumbnail_url, created_at, updated_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      courseId, title, courseSlug, description || null, technology_id || null,\n      semester || null, level || null, price_bdt || 0, is_published ? 1 : 0,\n      instructorId, thumbnail_url || null, now, now\n    ).run();\n\n    // Auto-create course_instructors junction entry\n    try {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        INSERT INTO course_instructors (course_id, instructor_id, sort_order, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, 0, ?)\n      `).bind(courseId, instructorId, now).run();\n    } catch {}\n\n    // Auto-create a \"single\" course_package with the same price\n    try {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        INSERT INTO course_packages (course_id, name, price_bdt, original_price, package_type, features, is_active, sort_order, created_at, updated_at)\n        VALUES (?, 'Single', ?, ?, 'single', '', 1, 0, ?, ?)\n      `).bind(courseId, price_bdt || 0, price_bdt || 0, now, now).run();\n    } catch {}\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare('SELECT * FROM courses WHERE id = ?').bind(courseId).first();\n    const course = formatCourseRow(row as Record<string, unknown>);\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, course }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// PUT /courses/:id \u2014 Update course (only if instructor owns it)\ninstructorRoutes.put('/courses/:id', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const courseId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Verify ownership\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n\n    const fieldMapping: Record<string, string> = {\n      title: 'title',\n      slug: 'slug',\n      description: 'description',\n      technology_id: 'technology_id',\n      technologyId: 'technology_id',\n      semester: 'semester',\n      level: 'level',\n      price_bdt: 'price_bdt',\n      priceBdt: 'price_bdt',\n      is_published: 'is_published',\n      isPublished: 'is_published',\n      thumbnail_url: 'thumbnail_url',\n      thumbnailUrl: 'thumbnail_url',\n    };\n\n    const setClauses: string[] = [];\n    const params: unknown[] = [];\n\n    for (const [bodyField, dbColumn] of Object.entries(fieldMapping)) {\n      if (body[bodyField] !== undefined) {\n        setClauses.push(`${dbColumn} = ?`);\n        params.push(body[bodyField]);\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (setClauses.length === 0) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'No valid fields to update' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    setClauses.push('updated_at = ?');\n    params.push(new Date().toISOString());\n    params.push(courseId);\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `UPDATE courses SET ${setClauses.join(', ')} WHERE id = ?`\n    ).bind(...params).run();\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare('SELECT * FROM courses WHERE id = ?').bind(courseId).first();\n    const course = formatCourseRow(row as Record<string, unknown>);\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, course });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// CHAPTERS CRUD (within courses instructor owns)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// GET /courses/:courseId/chapters \u2014 List chapters for a course\ninstructorRoutes.get('/courses/:courseId/chapters', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const courseId = c.req.param('courseId');\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM chapters WHERE course_id = ? ORDER BY sort_order ASC'\n    ).bind(courseId).all();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, chapters: result.results });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST /courses/:courseId/chapters \u2014 Create chapter (verify ownership)\ninstructorRoutes.post('/courses/:courseId/chapters', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const courseId = c.req.param('courseId');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Verify ownership\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { title, slug, description, subject_id, sort_order } = body;\n\n    if (!title) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'title is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const chapterId = generateId();\n    const chapterSlug = slug || slugify(title);\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO chapters (id, course_id, subject_id, title, slug, description, sort_order, is_active, created_at, updated_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 1, ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      chapterId, courseId, subject_id || null, title, chapterSlug,\n      description || null, sort_order || 0, now, now\n    ).run();\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare('SELECT * FROM chapters WHERE id = ?').bind(chapterId).first();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, chapter: row }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// PUT /chapters/:id \u2014 Update chapter (verify the chapter's course_id belongs to instructor)\ninstructorRoutes.put('/chapters/:id', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const chapterId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Get chapter to find its course_id\n    const existing = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT course_id FROM chapters WHERE id = ?'\n    ).bind(chapterId).first<{ course_id: string }>();\n\n    if (!existing) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Chapter not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    // Verify ownership of the course\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, existing.course_id, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n\n    const fieldMapping: Record<string, string> = {\n      title: 'title',\n      slug: 'slug',\n      description: 'description',\n      subject_id: 'subject_id',\n      subjectId: 'subject_id',\n      sort_order: 'sort_order',\n      sortOrder: 'sort_order',\n      is_active: 'is_active',\n      isActive: 'is_active',\n    };\n\n    const setClauses: string[] = [];\n    const params: unknown[] = [];\n\n    for (const [bodyField, dbColumn] of Object.entries(fieldMapping)) {\n      if (body[bodyField] !== undefined) {\n        setClauses.push(`${dbColumn} = ?`);\n        params.push(body[bodyField]);\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (setClauses.length === 0) {\n      return c.json({ c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { category, subject, description, priority } = body;\n\n    if (!category || !subject || !description) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'category, subject, and description are required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO support_tickets (user_id, category, subject, description, priority, status, created_at, updated_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'open', ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      instructorId, category, subject, description,\n      priority || 'medium', now, now\n    ).run();\n\n    const insertedId = result.meta?.last_row_id;\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_tickets WHERE rowid = ?'\n    ).bind(insertedId).first();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, ticket: row }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST /support/tickets/:id/messages \u2014 Send message on support ticket\ninstructorRoutes.post('/support/tickets/:id/messages', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const ticketId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Verify the ticket belongs to this instructor\n    const ticket = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT user_id, status FROM support_tickets WHERE id = ?'\n    ).bind(ticketId).first<{ user_id: string; status: string }>();\n\n    if (!ticket) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Ticket not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    if (ticket.user_id !== instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You can only message on your own tickets' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { message } = body;\n\n    if (!message) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'message is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO support_messages (ticket_id, user_id, message, is_admin, created_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, 0, ?)\n    `).bind(ticketId, instructorId, message, now).run();\n\n    // Update ticket status to 'waiting' if it was 'replied' or 'resolved'\n    if (ticket.status !== 'open') {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        \"UPDATE support_tickets SET status = 'waiting', updated_at = ? WHERE id = ?\"\n      ).bind(now, ticketId).run();\n    } else {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'UPDATE support_tickets SET updated_at = ? WHERE id = ?'\n      ).bind(now, ticketId).run();\n    }\n\n    const insertedId = result.meta?.last_row_id;\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_messages WHERE rowid = ?'\n    ).bind(insertedId).first();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, message: row }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// COURSE THUMBNAIL UPLOAD (FormData to R2)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// POST /courses/:id/thumbnail \u2014 Upload course thumbnail\ninstructorRoutes.post('/courses/:id/thumbnail', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const courseId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Verify ownership\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const formData = await c.req.formData();\n    const fileEntry = formData.get('thumbnail');\n    if (!fileEntry || typeof fileEntry === 'string') {\n      return c.json({ error: 'No thumbnail file provided' }, 400);\n    }\n    const file = fileEntry as unknown as Blob & { name?: string; type?: string };\n\n    // Upload to R2_THUMBNAILS bucket\n    const key = `courses/${courseId}/${Date.now()}-${file.name || 'thumbnail'}`;\n    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();\n    await c.env.R2_THUMBNAILS.put(key, arrayBuffer, {\n      httpMetadata: { contentType: file.type || 'image/jpeg' },\n    });\n\n    const thumbnailUrl = await getPublicUrl(c.env, 'thumbnails', key);\n\n    // Update course thumbnail_url in D1\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'UPDATE courses SET thumbnail_url = ?, updated_at = ? WHERE id = ?'\n    ).bind(thumbnailUrl, new Date().toISOString(), courseId).run();\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, thumbnail_url: thumbnailUrl });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// VIDEO UPLOAD WITH FORMDATA (video file + thumbnail + CC)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\n// POST /courses/:courseId/videos/upload \u2014 Upload video with FormData (video file, thumbnail, CC)\ninstructorRoutes.post('/courses/:courseId/videos/upload', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authRole = c.get('authRole');\n    const instructorId = authRole === 'admin' ? c.req.query('instructorId')! : c.get('instructorId');\n    const courseId = c.req.param('courseId');\n\n    if (!instructorId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'instructorId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Verify ownership\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const formData = await c.req.formData();\n\n    // Metadata fields\n    const title = formData.get('title') as string;\n    const chapter_id = (formData.get('chapter_id') as string) || null;\n    const subject_id = (formData.get('subject_id') as string) || null;\n    const lesson_type = (formData.get('lesson_type') as string) || 'video';\n    const sort_order = parseInt(formData.get('sort_order') as string) || 0;\n    const is_preview = formData.get('is_preview') === '1' ? 1 : 0;\n    const is_published = formData.get('is_published') === '1' ? 1 : 0;\n    const duration = parseInt(formData.get('duration') as string) || 0;\n    const description = (formData.get('description') as string) || null;\n\n    if (!title) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'title is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    let videoUrl = '';\n    let thumbnailUrl = '';\n    let ccUrl = '';\n\n    // Upload video file to R2_VIDEOS\n    const videoEntry = formData.get('video');\n    if (videoEntry && typeof videoEntry !== 'string') {\n      const videoFile = videoEntry as unknown as Blob & { name?: string; type?: string };\n      const videoKey = `courses/${courseId}/videos/${Date.now()}-${videoFile.name || 'video.mp4'}`;\n      const videoBuffer = await videoFile.arrayBuffer();\n      await c.env.R2_VIDEOS.put(videoKey, videoBuffer, {\n        httpMetadata: { contentType: videoFile.type || 'video/mp4' },\n      });\n      videoUrl = await getPublicUrl(c.env, 'videos', videoKey);\n    } else {\n      // Check for external URL\n      const externalUrl = formData.get('video_url') as string;\n      if (externalUrl) {\n        videoUrl = externalUrl;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Upload thumbnail file to R2_THUMBNAILS\n    const thumbEntry = formData.get('thumbnail');\n    if (thumbEntry && typeof thumbEntry !== 'string') {\n      const thumbFile = thumbEntry as unknown as Blob & { name?: string; type?: string };\n      const thumbKey = `courses/${courseId}/thumbnails/${Date.now()}-${thumbFile.name || 'thumbnail.jpg'}`;\n      const thumbBuffer = await thumbFile.arrayBuffer();\n      await c.env.R2_THUMBNAILS.put(thumbKey, thumbBuffer, {\n        httpMetadata: { contentType: thumbFile.type || 'image/jpeg' },\n      });\n      thumbnailUrl = await getPublicUrl(c.env, 'thumbnails', thumbKey);\n    }\n\n    // Upload CC/subtitle file to R2_RESOURCES\n    const ccEntry = formData.get('cc_file');\n    if (ccEntry && typeof ccEntry !== 'string') {\n      const ccFile = ccEntry as unknown as Blob & { name?: string; type?: string };\n      const ccKey = `courses/${courseId}/subtitles/${Date.now()}-${ccFile.name || 'subtitles.vtt'}`;\n      const ccBuffer = await ccFile.arrayBuffer();\n      await c.env.R2_RESOURCES.put(ccKey, ccBuffer, {\n        httpMetadata: { contentType: ccFile.type || 'text/vtt' },\n      });\n      ccUrl = await getPublicUrl(c.env, 'resources', ccKey);\n    }\n\n    // Create video record in D1\n    const videoId = generateId();\n    const videoSlug = slugify(title);\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO videos (id, course_id, title, slug, video_url, thumbnail_url, duration, sort_order, is_preview, is_published, chapter_id, subject_id, lesson_type, created_at, updated_at)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      videoId, courseId, title, videoSlug, videoUrl || null,\n      thumbnailUrl || null, duration, sort_order, is_preview, is_published,\n      chapter_id, subject_id, lesson_type || null, now, now\n    ).run();\n\n    // If there's a CC URL, store it in course_resources as subtitle\n    if (ccUrl) {\n      const resourceId = generateId();\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        INSERT INTO course_resources (id, course_id, chapter_id, lesson_id, title, description, file_url, file_type, sort_order, uploaded_by, created_at, updated_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 0, ?, ?, ?)\n      `).bind(\n        resourceId, courseId, chapter_id, videoId,\n        `${title} - Subtitles`, 'Closed captions / subtitles',\n        ccUrl, 'vtt', instructorId, now, now\n      ).run();\n    }\n\n    const row = await c.env.DB.prepare('SELECT * FROM videos WHERE id = ?').bind(videoId).first();\n    const video = formatVideoRow(row as Record<string, unknown>);\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, video, cc_url: ccUrl || undefined }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// TECHNOLOGIES & SUBJECTS (read-only for instructor)\n// GET /technologies \u2014 List all technologies (for course creation dropdowns)\ninstructorRoutes.get('/technologies', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const result = await error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /subjects \u2014 List subjects (optionally filter by technology_id)\ninstructorRoutes.get('/subjects', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const technologyId = c.req.query('technology_id');\n    let query = 'SELECT * FROM subjects';\n    const params: unknown[] = [];\n\n    if (technologyId) {\n      query += ' WHERE technology_id = ?';\n      params.push(parseInt(technologyId));\n    }\n\n    query += ' ORDER BY sort_order ASC, name ASC';\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(query).bind(...params).all();\n    return c.json({ success: true, subjects: result.results });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /courses/:id/subjects \u2014 Get subjects assigned to a course\ninstructorRoutes.get('/courses/:id/subjects', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const courseId = c.req.param('id');\n    const { instructorId, error: idError } = getInstructorId(c);\n    if (idError) return idError;\n\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    let subjects: any[] = [];\n    try {\n      const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        SELECT cs.*, s.name as subject_name, s.slug as subject_slug, s.technology_id\n        FROM course_subjects cs\n        LEFT JOIN subjects s ON cs.subject_id = s.id\n        WHERE cs.course_id = ?\n        ORDER BY cs.sort_order ASC\n      `).bind(courseId).all();\n      subjects = result.results as any[];\n    } catch {}\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, subjects });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST /courses/:id/subjects \u2014 Add subject to course\ninstructorRoutes.post('/courses/:id/subjects', instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const courseId = c.req.param('id');\n    const { instructorId, error: idError } = getInstructorId(c);\n    if (idError) return idError;\n\n    const owns = await verifyCourseOwnership(c.env, courseId, instructorId);\n    if (!owns) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'You do not own this course' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n    const { subject_id, sort_order } = body;\n\n    if (!subject_id) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'subject_id is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    try {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        INSERT INTO course_subjects (course_id, subject_id, sort_order, created_at)\n        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\n      `).bind(courseId, subject_id, sort_order || 0, now).run();\n    } catch (err: any) {\n      if (err?.message?.includes('UNIQUE') || err?.message?.includes('duplicate')) {\n        return c.json({ error: 'Subject already added to this course' }, 400);\n      }\n    }\n\n    return c.json({ success: true, message: 'Subject added to course' }, 201);\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ instructorOrAdminMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const courseId = c.req.param('id');\n    const subjectId = c.req.param('subjectId');\n    const { instructorId, error: idError } = Provide Authorization: Bearer <token>' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n  if (!token) {\n    return c.json({ error: 'Invalid token' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const result = await validateInstructorSession(c.env, token);\n\n    if (!result.authorized) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Invalid or expired instructor session' }, 401);\n    }\n\n    c.set('instructorId', result.userId!);\n    c.set('instructorEmail', result.email || '');\n    c.set('instructorName', result.name || '');\n    c.set('instructorAvatarUrl', result.avatarUrl || '');\n\n    await next();\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Instructor auth middleware error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: 'Authentication failed' }, 401);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Composite auth middleware \u2014 tries instructor session first, falls back to admin session\n * Sets c.set('authRole', 'instructor' | 'admin') plus the corresponding user variables\n */\nexport async function instructorOrAdminMiddleware(\n  c: Context<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: InstructorOrAdminAuthVariables }>,\n  next: Next\n) {\n  const authHeader = c.req.header('Authorization');\n\n  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {\n    return c.json({ error: 'Authentication required. Provide Authorization: Bearer <token>' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n  if (!token) {\n    return c.json({ error: 'Invalid token' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  try {\n    // Try instructor session first\n    const instructorResult = await validateInstructorSession(c.env, token);\n\n    if (instructorResult.authorized) {\n      c.set('authRole', 'instructor');\n      c.set('instructorId', instructorResult.userId!);\n      c.set('instructorEmail', instructorResult.email || '');\n      c.set('instructorName', instructorResult.name || '');\n      c.set('instructorAvatarUrl', instructorResult.avatarUrl || '');\n      await next();\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Fall back to admin session\n    const adminSession = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT id, user_id, email, name, role, expires_at, is_active FROM admin_sessions WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    )\n      .bind(token)\n      .first<{ id: string; user_id: string; email: string; name: string; role: string; expires_at: string; is_active: number }>();\n\n    if (!adminSession) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Invalid or expired session' }, 401);\n    }\n\n    // Check admin session expiration\n    const expiresAt = new Date(adminSession.expires_at);\n    if (expiresAt < new Date()) {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'UPDATE admin_sessions SET is_active = 0 WHERE id = ?'\n      ).bind(token).run();\n      return c.json({ error: 'Session expired. Please login again.' }, 401);\n    }\n\n    c.set('authRole', 'admin');\n    c.set('instructorId', ''); // Admin doesn't have instructor ID by default\n    c.set('instructorEmail', adminSession.email);\n    c.set('instructorName', adminSession.name || '');\n    c.set('instructorAvatarUrl', '');\n    c.set('adminId', adminSession.user_id);\n    c.set('adminEmail', adminSession.email);\n    c.set('adminName', adminSession.name || '');\n\n    await next();\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Instructor or admin auth middleware error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: 'Authentication failed' }, 401);\n  }\n}\n", "/**\n * Instructor authentication for DAKKHO Instructor API\n * Validates instructor sessions against D1 instructor_sessions table\n * Also provides composite middleware that accepts instructor OR admin sessions\n */\n\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport { generateId, getSessionExpiry } from './utils';\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Instructor Session CRUD \u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Validate an instructor session token\n * Returns authorized status and user info if valid\n */\nexport async function validateInstructorSession(\n  env: Env,\n  token: string\n): Promise<{ authorized: boolean; userId?: string; email?: string; name?: string; avatarUrl?: string }> {\n  try {\n    const session = await env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT user_id, email, name, avatar_url, expires_at, is_active FROM instructor_sessions WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    )\n      .bind(token)\n      .first<{ user_id: string; email: string; name: string | null; avatar_url: string | null; expires_at: string; is_active: number }>();\n\n    if (!session) {\n      return { authorized: false };\n    }\n\n    // Check expiration\n    const expiresAt = new Date(session.expires_at);\n    if (expiresAt < new Date()) {\n      await env.DB.prepare(\n        'UPDATE instructor_sessions SET is_active = 0 WHERE id = ?'\n      ).bind(token).run();\n      return { authorized: false };\n    }\n\n    return {\n      authorized: true,\n      userId: session.user_id,\n      email: session.email,\n      name: session.name || undefined,\n      avatarUrl: session.avatar_url || undefined,\n    };\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Instructor session validation error:', error);\n    return { authorized: false };\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Create a new instructor session\n * Returns the session token (ID)\n */\nexport async function createInstructorSession(\n  env: Env,\n  userId: string,\n  email: string,\n  name: string,\n  ipAddress?: string,\n  deviceInfo?: string,\n  avatarUrl?: string\n): Promise<string> {\n  const sessionId = generateId();\n  const expiresAt = getSessionExpiry(7); from 'hono';\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport type { AuthVariables } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { adminAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { DEFAULT_CONFIG, type ServerConfig } from '../lib/types';\nimport { logAudit } from '../lib/audit';\nimport { getErrorMessage } from '../lib/utils';\n\nconst configRoutes = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: AuthVariables }>();\n\n// Apply auth middleware to all config routes\nconfigRoutes.use('*', adminAuthMiddleware);\n\n// GET / \u2014 Get current config\nconfigRoutes.get('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    // First try KV cache\n    const cachedConfig = await c.env.KV_CONFIG.get('server_config', 'json');\n    if (cachedConfig) {\n      return c.json(cachedConfig);\n    }\n\n    // Fall back to D1\n    const { results } = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT key, value FROM app_config'\n    ).all<{ key: string; value: string }>();\n\n    const configMap: Record<string, unknown> = {};\n    for (const row of results) {\n      try {\n        configMap[row.key] = JSON.parse(row.value);\n      } catch {\n        configMap[row.key] = row.value;\n      }\n    }\n\n    const config: ServerConfig = {\n      featureToggles: { ...DEFAULT_CONFIG.featureToggles, ...(configMap.featureToggles as Partial<ServerConfig['featureToggles']>) },\n      homePageSections: (configMap.homePageSections as ServerConfig['homePageSections']) || DEFAULT_CONFIG.homePageSections,\n      sidebarVisibility: { ...DEFAULT_CONFIG.sidebarVisibility, ...(configMap.sidebarVisibility as Partial<ServerConfig['sidebarVisibility']>) },\n      bottomNavTabs: (configMap.bottomNavTabs as ServerConfig['bottomNavTabs']) || DEFAULT_CONFIG.bottomNavTabs,\n      topBarElements: { ...DEFAULT_CONFIG.topBarElements, ...(configMap.topBarElements as Partial<ServerConfig['topBarElements']>) },\n      cardStyle: (configMap.cardStyle as ServerConfig['cardStyle']) || DEFAULT_CONFIG.cardStyle,\n      contentProtection: { ...DEFAULT_CONFIG.contentProtection, ...(configMap.contentProtection as Partial<ServerConfig['contentProtection']>) },\n    };\n\n    // Cache in KV\n    await c.env.KV_CONFIG.put('server_config', JSON.stringify(config), { expirationTtl: 300 });\n\n    return c.json(config);\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// PUT / \u2014 Update config\nconfigRoutes.put('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const config = await c.req.json<ServerConfig>();\n\n    const bottomNavTabs: config.bottomNavTabs,\n      topBarElements: config.topBarElements,\n      cardStyle: config.cardStyle,\n      contentProtection: config.contentProtection,\n    };\n\n    // Upsert each section into D1\n    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(sections)) {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        `INSERT INTO app_config (key, value, updated_at) VALUES (?, ?, datetime('now'))\n         ON CONFLICT(key) DO UPDATE SET value = excluded.value, updated_at = datetime('now')`\n      )\n        .bind(key, JSON.stringify(value))\n        .run();\n    }\n\n    // Update KV cache (replaces MQTT broadcast)\n    await c.env.KV_CONFIG.put('server_config', JSON.stringify(config));\n    // Set a config-updated timestamp so clients can poll for changes\n    await c.env.KV_CONFIG.put('config_updated_at', new Date().toISOString());\n\n    const user = c.get('user');\n    await logAudit(c.env, user.id, 'UPDATE_CONFIG', 'config', undefined, config);\n\n    return homePageSections: config.homePageSections,\n      sidebarVisibility: config.sidebarVisibility,\n      bottomNavTabs: config.bottomNavTabs,\n      topBarElements: config.topBarElements,\n \u2500\u2500\u2500 Service Status Types \u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface ServiceStatus {\n  status: 'connected' | 'error' | 'limited';\n  message?: string;\n}\n", "/**\n * Notifications routes \u2014 GET, POST\n * D1-only: All notifications stored in D1 notifications table + notification_logs\n * Also sends OneSignal push notifications\n *\n * Category-based notification delivery:\n * - Admin selects a category when sending notification\n * - If user has that category OFF \u2192 skip user entirely (no in-app, no push)\n * - If user has category ON + quiet hours active \u2192 in-app only (no push sound)\n * - If user has category ON + no quiet hours \u2192 in-app + push with sound\n */\n\nimport { Hono } from 'hono';\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport type { AuthVariables } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { adminAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { logAudit } from '../lib/audit';\nimport { getErrorMessage } from '../lib/utils';\nimport { sendPushNotification, getUserPushTokens, getBatchUserPushTokens } from '../lib/onesignal';\n\nconst notificationRoutes = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: AuthVariables }>();\n\n// Apply auth middleware to all notification routes\nnotificationRoutes.use('*', adminAuthMiddleware);\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Helper: Check if current time is within user's quiet hours \u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction isInQuietHours(\n  quietHoursEnabled: boolean,\n  quietStart: string,\n  quietEnd: string\n): boolean {\n  if (!quietHoursEnabled) return false;\n\n  const now = new Date();\n  const currentMinutes = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();\n\n  const [startH, startM] = (quietStart || '22:00').split(':').map(Number);\n  const [endH, endM] = (quietEnd || '08:00').split(':').map(Number);\n\n  const startMinutes = (startH || 0) * 60 + (startM || 0);\n  const endMinutes = (endH || 0) * 60 + (endM || 0);\n\n  // Handle overnight quiet hours (e.g., 22:00 \u2192 08:00)\n  if (startMinutes > endMinutes) {\n    // e.g., 22:00 to 08:00 \u2014 current time is in quiet hours if >= 22:00 OR < 08:00\n    return currentMinutes >= startMinutes || currentMinutes < endMinutes;\n  } else {\n    // e.g., 12:00 to 14:00 \u2014 current time is in quiet hours if >= start AND < end\n    return currentMinutes >= startMinutes && currentMinutes < endMinutes;\n  }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Helper: Map notification type/category to preference columns \u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction getCategoryPushColumn(category: string): string {\n  const map: Record<string, string> = {\n    'course-update': 'course_updates_push',\n    'info': 'course_updates_push',\n    'success': 'course_updates_push',\n    'grades': 'grades_push',\n    'schedule': 'schedule_push',\n    'payment': 'payment_push',\n    'announcement': 'promotions_push',\n    'promotions': 'promotions_push',\n    'social': 'social_push',\n    'system': 'system_push',\n    'warning': 'system_push',\n    'error': 'system_push',\n    'support': 'system_push',\n  };\n  return map[category] || map['info'];\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Helper: Get user notification preferences for a given category \u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Returns: { shouldDeliver: boolean, shouldPush: boolean }\nasync function checkDeliveryPrefs(\n  env: Env,\n  userId: string,\n  category: string\n): Promise<{ shouldDeliver: boolean; shouldPush: boolean }> {\n  try {\n    const prefs = await env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM notification_preferences WHERE user_id = ?'\n    ).bind(userId).first() as any;\n\n    if (!prefs) {\n      // No preferences set \u2192 deliver with push by default\n      return { shouldDeliver: true, shouldPush: true };\n    }\n\n    // Check master push switch\n    if (!prefs.push_enabled) {\n      // Master push is off \u2014 still deliver in-app, but no push\n      // But check if category itself is off\n      const categoryCol = getCategoryPushColumn(category);\n      const categoryEnabled = !!prefs[categoryCol];\n      if (!categoryEnabled) {\n        // Category is off \u2192 don't deliver at all\n        return { shouldDeliver: false, shouldPush: false };\n      }\n      // Category is on, master push is off \u2192 in-app only\n      return { shouldDeliver: true, shouldPush: false };\n    }\n\n    // Check per-category preference\n    const categoryCol = getCategoryPushColumn(category);\n    const categoryEnabled = !!prefs[categoryCol];\n    if (!categoryEnabled) {\n      // Category is off \u2192 don't deliver at all\n      return { shouldDeliver: false, shouldPush: false };\n    }\n\n    // Category is on \u2014 check quiet hours\n    const quietHoursEnabled = !!prefs.quiet_hours_enabled;\n    if (isInQuietHours(quietHoursEnabled, prefs.quiet_hours_start, prefs.quiet_hours_end)) {\n      // Quiet hours active \u2192 deliver in-app silently, no push\n      return { shouldDeliver: true, shouldPush: false };\n    }\n\n    // All good \u2192 deliver with push\n    return { shouldDeliver: true, shouldPush: true };\n  } catch (error) {\n    // On error, default to delivering with push\n    console.error('Failed to check delivery prefs:', error);\n    return { shouldDeliver: true, shouldPush: true };\n  }\n}\n\n// GET / \u2014 List notifications\nnotificationRoutes.get('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const page = parseInt(c.req.query('page') || '1');\n    const limit = parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '20');\n    const userId = c.req.query('userId') || '';\n    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;\n\n    let where = 'WHERE 1=1';\n    const params: unknown[] = [];\n\n    if (userId) {\n      where += ' AND user_id = ?';\n      params.push(userId);\n    }\n\n    // Count total\n    const countResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM notifications ${where}`\n    ).bind(...params).first();\n    const total = (countResult as any)?.total || 0;\n\n    // Get notifications\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT * FROM notifications ${where} ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`\n    ).bind(...params, limit, offset).all();\n\n    // Also get notification logs for broadcast/sent info\n    const logsResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      \"SELECT * FROM notification_logs ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?\"\n    ).bind(limit, offset).all();\n\n    // Combine results\n    const documents = [\n      ...(result.results as any[]).map(row => ({\n        id: row.id,\n        title: row.title,\n        message: row.message,\n        type: row.type || 'info',\n        category: row.category || '',\n        userId: row.user_id,\n        isRead: !!row.read,\n        actionUrl: row.action_url,\n        createdAt: row.created_at,\n        source: 'd1',\n      })),\n      ...(logsResult.results as any[]).map(row => ({\n        id: `log-${row.id}`,\n        title: row.title,\n        message: row.message,\n        type: row.metadata ? (JSON.parse(row.metadata || '{}').notifType || 'info') : 'info',\n        category: row.category || '',\n        targetType: row.target_type,\n        targetId: row.target_id,\n        sentCount: row.sent_count,\n        failedCount: row.failed_count,\n        createdAt: row.created_at,\n        source: 'log',\n      })),\n    ];\n\n    // Sort combined by date\n    documents.sort((a, b) => new Date(String(b.createdAt)).getTime() - new Date(String(a.createdAt)).getTime());\n\n    return c.json({ documents: documents.slice(0, limit), total: Math.max(total, documents.length) });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST / \u2014 Send notification(s)\nnotificationRoutes.post('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const data = await c.req.json<{\n      title: string;\n      message: string;\n      type?: string;\n      category?: string;\n      targetAll?: boolean;\n      targetUserId?: string;\n      targetInstitute?: string;\n      targetTechnology?: string;\n      actionUrl?: string;\n      [key: string]: unknown;\n    }>();\n\n    const {\n      title, message, type = 'info', category = 'info',\n      targetAll, targetUserId, targetInstitute, targetTechnology,\n      actionUrl, ...extraData\n    } = data;\n\n    if (!title || !message) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Title and message are required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // The effective category for preference matching is the type or explicit category\n    const effectiveCategory = category || type;\n\n    const created: Record<string, unknown>[] = [];\n    const skippedByPref: string[] = [];  // Users skipped because category is OFF\n    const silentDelivery: string[] = [];  // Users getting silent (quiet hours) delivery\n    const pushDelivery: string[] = [];    // Users getting push notification\n    let failedCount = 0;\n    let targetType = 'user';\n    let targetId = targetUserId || '';\n\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Helper: Process a single user's notification \u2500\u2500\u2500\n    async function processUser(userId: string): Promise<void> {\n      // Check delivery preferences for this user\n      const { shouldDeliver, shouldPush } = await checkDeliveryPrefs(c.env, userId, effectiveCategory);\n\n      if (!shouldDeliver) {\n        // User has this category OFF \u2014 skip entirely\n        skippedByPref.push(userId);\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // Create in-app notification\n      try {\n        const notifId = crypto.randomUUID();\n        await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n          INSERT INTO notifications (id, user_id, title, message, type, category, read, action_url)\n          VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 0, ?)\n        `).bind(notifId, userId, title, message, type, effectiveCategory, actionUrl || null).run();\n        created.push({ id: notifId, userId });\n      } catch (docErr) {\n        failedCount++;\n        console.error('Failed to create notification for user:', userId, getErrorMessage(docErr));\n        return;\n      }\n\n      if (shouldPush) {\n        pushDelivery.push(userId);\n      } else {\n        silentDelivery.push(userId);\n      }\n    }\n\n    if (targetAll) {\n      targetType = 'all';\n      targetId = 'all';\n      // Send to all users \u2014 paginate through users\n      let offset = 0;\n      const batchLimit = 100;\n      let hasMore = true;\n\n      while (hasMore) {\n        const usersResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n          'SELECT id FROM users WHERE is_active = 1 LIMIT ? OFFSET ?'\n        ).bind(batchLimit, offset).all();\n\n        for (const user of usersResult.results as { id: string }[]) {\n          await processUser(user.id);\n        }\n\n        offset += batchLimit;\n        hasMore = usersResult.results.length === batchLimit;\n      }\n    } else if (targetInstitute) {\n      targetType = 'institute';\n      targetId = targetInstitute;\n      // Send to all users in an institute\n      const usersResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT id FROM users WHERE institute_id = ? AND is_active = 1 LIMIT 500'\n      ).bind(targetInstitute).all();\n\n      for (const user of usersResult.results as { id: string }[]) {\n        await processUser(user.id);\n      }\n    } else if (targetTechnology) {\n      targetType = 'technology';\n      targetId = targetTechnology;\n      // Send to all users with a specific technology\n      const usersResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT id FROM users WHERE technology = ? AND is_active = 1 LIMIT 500'\n      ).bind(targetTechnology).all();\n\n      for (const user of usersResult.results as { id: string }[]) {\n        await processUser(user.id);\n      }\n    } else if (targetUserId) {\n      // Send to specific user\n      await processUser(targetUserId);\n    } else {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Specify targetAll, targetUserId, targetInstitute, or targetTechnology' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500 Send OneSignal push notifications to eligible users \u2500\u2500\u2500\n    try {\n      if (pushDelivery.length > 0) {\n        // Send push to users who have push enabled and are not in quiet hours\n        const pushTokens = await getBatchUserPushTokens(c.env, pushDelivery);\n        if (pushTokens.length > 0) {\n          await sendPushNotification(c.env, {\n            title,\n            message,\n            targetPlayerIds: pushTokens,\n            url: actionUrl || undefined,\n          });\n        }\n      }\n\n      // For targetAll with no preferences set, also try segment-based push as fallback\n      if (targetAll && pushDelivery.length === 0 && skippedByPref.length === 0) {\n        await sendPushNotification(c.env, {\n          title,\n          message,\n          targetSegment: 'All',\n          url: actionUrl || undefined,\n        });\n      }\n    } catch (pushErr) {\n      console.error('Push notification failed:', getErrorMessage(pushErr));\n    }\n\n    // Log to notification_logs\n    const user = c.get('user');\n    const logMetadata = JSON.stringify({\n      notifType: type,\n      category: effectiveCategory,\n      actionUrl: actionUrl || '',\n      skippedByPref: skippedByPref.length,\n      silentDelivery: silentDelivery.length,\n      pushDelivery: pushDelivery.length,\n      ...extraData,\n    });\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO notification_logs (type, category, title, message, target_type, target_id, sent_count, failed_count, metadata, created_by)\n      VALUES ('in-app', ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n    `).bind(\n      effectiveCategory,\n      title,\n      message,\n      targetType,\n      targetId,\n      created.length,\n      failedCount,\n      logMetadata,\n      user.id\n    ).run();\n\n    await logAudit(c.env, user.id, 'SEND_NOTIFICATION', 'notifications', undefined, {\n      targetType,\n      targetId,\n      targetAll,\n      targetUserId,\n      targetInstitute,\n      targetTechnology,\n      category: effectiveCategory,\n      sentCount: created.length,\n      failedCount,\n      skippedByPref: skippedByPref.length,\n      silentDelivery: silentDelivery.length,\n      pushDelivery: pushDelivery.length,\n    });\n\n    return c.json({\n      created,\n      count: created.length,\n      failedCount,\n      skippedByPref: skippedByPref.length,\n      silentDelivery: silentDelivery.length,\n      pushDelivery: pushDelivery.length,\n      logged: true,\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\nexport default notificationRoutes;\n", "/**\n * OneSignal Push Notification integration for DAKKHO\n * Handles push notification sending and token management\n */\n\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport { generateId } from './utils';\n\ninterface PushNotificationPayload {\n  title: string;\n  titleBn?: string;\n  message: string;\n  messageBn?: string;\n  url?: string;\n  data?: Record<string, unknown>;\n  targetPlayerIds?: string[];\n  targetSegment?: string;\n}\n\ninterface PushNotificationResult {\n  success: boolean;\n  recipients: number;\n  errors: string[];\n}\n\n/**\n * Send a push notification via OneSignal\n */\nexport async function sendPushNotification(\n  env: Env,\n  payload: PushNotificationPayload\n): Promise<PushNotificationResult> {\n  try {\n    const appId = env.ONE_SIGNAL_APP_ID;\n    const restApiKey = env.ONE_SIGNAL_REST_API_KEY;\n\n    if (!appId || !restApiKey) {\n      console.warn('OneSignal not configured \u2014 skipping push notification');\n      return { success: false, recipients: 0, errors: ['OneSignal not configured'] };\n    }\n\n    const body: Record<string, unknown> = {\n      app_id: appId,\n      headings: { en: payload.title, bn: payload.titleBn || payload.title },\n      contents: { en: payload.message, bn: payload.messageBn || payload.message },\n      data: payload.data || {},\n    };\n\n    if (payload.url) {\n      body.url = payload.url;\n    }\n\n    if (payload.targetPlayerIds && payload.targetPlayerIds.length > 0) {\n      body.include_player_ids = payload.targetPlayerIds;\n    } else if (payload.targetSegment) {\n      body.included_segments = [payload.targetSegment];\n    } else {\n      body.included_segments = ['All'];\n    }\n\n    const response = await fetch('https://onesignal.com/api/v1/notifications', {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: {\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json',\n        Authorization: `Basic ${restApiKey}`,\n      },\n      body: JSON.stringify(body),\n    });\n\n    const result = await response.json() as any;\n\n    if (response.ok) {\n      return {\n        success: true,\n        recipients: result.recipients || 0,\n        errors: result.errors || [],\n      };\n    } else {\n      return {\n        success: false,\n        recipients: 0,\n        errors: [result.errors?.[0] || 'Unknown OneSignal error'],\n      };\n    }\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('OneSignal push error:', error);\n    return {\n      success: false,\n      recipients: 0,\n      errors: [error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'],\n    };\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Get push tokens for a specific user\n */\nexport async function getUserPushTokens(\n  env: Env,\n  userId: string\n): Promise<string[]> {\n  try {\n    const result = await env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT push_token FROM user_push_tokens WHERE user_id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    ).bind(userId).all();\n\n    return result.results.map((row: any) => row.push_token);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to get user push tokens:', error);\n    return [];\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Get push tokens for multiple users (batch)\n */\nexport async function getBatchUserPushTokens(\n  env: Env,\n  userIds: string[]\n): Promise<string[]> {\n  if (userIds.length === 0) return [];\n\n  try {\n    const placeholders = userIds.map(() => '?').join(',');\n    const result = await env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT DISTINCT push_token FROM user_push_tokens WHERE user_id IN (${placeholders}) AND is_active = 1`\n    ).bind(...userIds).all();\n\n    return result.results.map((row: any) => row.push_token);\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to get batch user push tokens:', error);\n    return [];\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Register a push token for a user\n */\nexport async function registerPushToken(\n  env: Env,\n  userId: string,\n  pushToken: string,\n  deviceType?: string,\n  deviceInfo?: string\n): Promise<void> {\n  try {\n    // Upsert: deactivate existing tokens for this user+token combo, then insert\n    await env.DB.prepare(\n      'UPDATE user_push_tokens SET is_active = 1, updated_at = datetime(\\'now\\') WHERE user_id = ? AND push_token = ?'\n    ).bind(userId, pushToken).run();\n\n    // Try insert (will be ignored if already exists due to update above being sufficient)\n    await env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO user_push_tokens (id, user_id, push_token, device_type, device_info, is_active, created_at)\n      SELECT ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 1, datetime('now')\n      WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM user_push_tokens WHERE user_id = ? AND push_token = ?)\n    `).bind(generateId(), userId, pushToken, deviceType || null, deviceInfo || null, userId, pushToken).run();\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error('Failed to register push token:', error);\n    throw error;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Unregister a push token (deactivate it)\n */\nexport async function unregisterPushToken(\n  env: Env,\n  pushToken: string\n): Promise<void> {\n enabled and current time is within quiet hours.\n */\nexport async function checkUserNotifPrefs(\n  env: Env,\n  userId: string,\n  notifType: string\n): Promise<{ push: boolean; email: boolean; quietHours: boolean }> {\n  try {\n    const prefs = await env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM notification_preferences WHERE user_id = ?'\n    ).bind(userId).first() as any;\n\n    if (!prefs) {\n      // No preferences set \u2192 use defaults (push: true, email: true for most types)\n      return { push: true, email: true, quietHours: false };\n    }\n\n    // Check if quiet hours are active\n    let isQuietHours = false;\n    if (prefs.quiet_hours_enabled) {\n      const now = new Date();\n      const currentMinutes = now.getHours() * 60 + now.getMinutes();\n      const [startH, startM] = (prefs.quiet_hours_start || '22:00').split(':').map(Number);\n      const [endH, endM] = (prefs.quiet_hours_end || '08:00').split(':').map(Number);\n      const startMinutes = (startH || 0) * 60 + (startM || 0);\n      const endMinutes = (endH || 0) * 60 + (endM || 0);\n\n      if (startMinutes > endMinutes) {\n        isQuietHours = currentMinutes >= startMinutes || currentMinutes < endMinutes;\n      } else {\n        isQuietHours = currentMinutes >= startMinutes && currentMinutes < endMinutes;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Check master switches first\n    if (!prefs.push_enabled) return { push: false, email: !!prefs.email_enabled, quietHours: isQuietHours };\n    if (!prefs.email_enabled) return { push: !!prefs.push_enabled, email: false, quietHours: isQuietHours };\n\n    // Map notification type to per-category preference columns\n    const typeToColumn: Record<string, { push: string; email: string }> = {\n      'course-update': { push: 'course_updates_push', email: 'course_updates_email' },\n      'info': { push: 'course_updates_push', email: 'course_updates_email' },\n      'success': { push: 'course_updates_push', email: 'course_updates_email' },\n      'grades': { push: 'grades_push', email: 'grades_email' },\n      'schedule': { push: 'schedule_push', email: 'schedule_email' },\n      'payment': { push: 'payment_push', email: 'payment_email' },\n      'announcement': { push: 'promotions_push', email: 'promotions_email' },\n      'promotions': { push: 'promotions_push', email: 'promotions_email' },\n      'social': { push: 'social_push', email: 'social_email' },\n      'system': { push: 'system_push', email: 'system_email' },\n      'warning': { push: 'system_push', email: 'system_email' },\n      'error': { push: 'system_push', email: 'system_email' },\n      'support': { push: 'system_push', email: 'system_email' },\n    };\n\n    const mapping = typeToColumn[notifType] || typeToColumn['info'];\n    return {\n      push: !!prefs[mapping.push],\n      email: !!prefs[mapping.email],\n      quietHours: isQuietHours,\n    };\n  } catch (error) {\n    // On error, default to allowing notifications\n    return { push: true, AND is_active = 1'\n    ).bind(code).first();\n\n    if (!coupon) {\n      return c.json({ valid: false, error: 'Invalid coupon code' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const cp = coupon as any;\n    const now = new Date().toISOString();\n\n    if (cp.valid_from > now || cp.valid_until < now) {\n      return c.json({ valid: false, error: 'Coupon has expired or is not yet active' });\n    }\n\n    if (cp.usage_limit && cp.usage_count >= cp.usage_limit) {\n      return c.json({ valid: false, error: 'Coupon usage limit reached' });\n    }\n\n    return c.json({\n      valid: true,\n      coupon: {\n        code: cp.code,\n        discount_type: cp.discount_type,\n        discount_value: cp.discount_value,\n        max_discount: cp.max_discount,\n        min_purchase: cp.min_purchase,\n      },\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Course Packages \u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nstudentApiRoutes.get('/course-packages', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const courseId = c.req.query('courseId');\n    if (!courseId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'courseId required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Get course price\n    const course = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT id, price FROM courses WHERE id = ? AND is_published = 1'\n    ).bind(courseId).first<{ id: string; price: number }>();\n\n    if (!course) {\n      return c.json({ packages: [] });\n    }\n\n    let result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM course_packages WHERE course_id = ? AND is_active = 1 ORDER BY price ASC'\n    ).bind(courseId).all();\n\n    // Auto-generate Single & Duo packages if missing (always show both for paid courses)\n    if (course.price > 0) {\n      const existingTypes = new Set((result.results as any[]).map((p: any) => p.package_type));\n      let needsRefetch = false;\n\n      // Ensure Single package exists\n      if (!existingTypes.has('single')) {\n        await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n          INSERT INTO course_packages (course_id, package_type, price, duration_months, max_users, is_auto_assign, is_active, display_name, description)\n          VALUES (?, 'single', ?, 6, 1, 1, 1, 'Single', '1 \u099C\u09A8 \u0987\u0989\u099C\u09BE\u09B0\u09C7\u09B0 \u099C\u09A8\u09CD\u09AF')\n        `).bind(courseId, course.price).run();\n        needsRefetch = true;\n      }\n\n      // Ensure Duo package exists (original price + 15% extra)\n      if (!existingTypes.has('dual')) {\n        const duoPrice = Math.round(course.price * 1.15);\n        await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n          INSERT INTO course_packages (course_id, package_type, price, duration_months, max_users, is_auto_assign, is_active, display_name, description)\n          VALUES (?, 'dual', ?, 6, 2, 1, 1, 'Duo', '2 \u099C\u09A8 \u0987\u0989\u099C\u09BE\u09B0\u09C7\u09B0 \u099C\u09A8\u09CD\u09AF \u2014 \u09AC\u09A8\u09CD\u09A7\u09C1\u0995\u09C7 \u09B6\u09C7\u09AF\u09BC\u09BE\u09B0 \u0995\u09B0\u09C1\u09A8!')\n        `).bind(courseId, duoPrice).run();\n        needsRefetch = true;\n      }\n\n      // Re-fetch after auto-generation\n      if (needsRefetch) {\n        result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n          'SELECT * FROM course_packages WHERE course_id = ? AND is_active = 1 AND package_type IN (\\\"single\\\", \\\"dual\\\") ORDER BY price ASC'\n        ).bind(courseId).all();\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Filter to only show Single and Duo packages (hide any other types)\n    const filteredPackages = (result.results as any[]).filter((p: any) => p.package_type === 'single' || p.package_type === 'dual');\n\n    return c.json({ packages: filteredPackages });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /packages/mine \u2014 Get current user's purchased packages\nstudentApiRoutes.get('/packages/mine', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const auth = await getStudentAuth(c);\n    if (!auth.authorized) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 401);\n    }\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      SELECT up.*, cp.package_type, cp.price, cp.duration_months, cp.course_id, cp.max_users,\n             c.title as course_title, c.thumbnail_url as course_thumbnail\n      FROM user_packages up\n      JOIN course_packages cp ON up.package_id = cp.id\n      LEFT JOIN courses c ON cp.course_id = c.id\n      WHERE up.user_id = ?\n      ORDER BY up.activated_at DESC\n    `).bind(auth.userId).all();\n\n    return c.json({ packages: result.results });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /users/lookup?email=... \u2014 Look up a user by email (for duo member)\nstudentApiRoutes.get('/users/lookup', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const email = c.req.query('email');\n    if (!email) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'email query parameter required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const user = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT id, full_name, email, institute_id, technology, avatar_url FROM users WHERE email = ? OFFSET ?`\n    ).bind(...params, limit, offset).all();\n\n    // Enrich courses with auto-calculated duration from videos\n    const enrichedCourses = await Promise.all(result.results.map(async (course: any) => {\n      try {\n        const vidStats = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n          'SELECT COUNT(*) as count, COALESCE(SUM(duration), 0) as total_duration FROM videos WHERE course_id = ?'\n        ).bind(course.id).first();\n        const vc = (vidStats as any)?.count || 0;\n        const td = (vidStats as any)?.total_duration || 0;\n        const avg = vc > 0 ? Math.round(td / vc * 10) / 10 : 0;\n        return { ...course, duration: avg, total_videos: vc, total_video_duration: td };\n      } catch {\n        return course;\n      }\n    }));\n\n    return c.json({ courses: enrichedCourses, total });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\nstudentApiRoutes.get('/courses/:id', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const id = c.req.param('id');\n    const course = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM courses WHERE id = ? AND is_published = 1'\n    ).bind(id).first();\n\n    if (!course) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Course not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    // Fetch all instructors for this course via course_instructors join table\n    let instructors: unknown[] = [];\n    try {\n      const instResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT i.* FROM instructors i JOIN course_instructors ci ON i.id = ci.instructor_id WHERE ci.course_id = ? ORDER BY ci.sort_order ASC'\n      ).bind(id).all();\n      instructors = instResult.results;\n    } catch {\n      // course_instructors table may not exist or no entries \u2014 fallback empty\n    }\n\n    // Fetch learning points for this course\n    let learningPoints: unknown[] = [];\n    try {\n      const lpResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT id, point_text, sort_order FROM course_learning_points WHERE course_id = ? ORDER BY sort_order ASC'\n      ).bind(id).all();\n      learningPoints = lpResult.results;\n    } catch {\n      // course_learning_points table may not exist \u2014 fallback empty\n    }\n\n    // Fetch subjects for this course via course_subjects join table\n    let subjects: unknown[] = [];\n    try {\n      const subResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT s.* FROM subjects s JOIN course_subjects cs ON s.id = cs.subject_id WHERE cs.course_id = ? ORDER BY cs.sort_order ASC'\n      ).bind(id).all();\n      subjects = subResult.results;\n    } catch {\n      // course_subjects or subjects table may not exist \u2014 fallback empty\n    }\n\n    // Auto-calculate duration from videos\n    let videoStats: any = null;\n    try {\n      videoStats = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT COUNT(*) as count, COALESCE(SUM(duration), 0) as total_duration FROM videos WHERE course_id = ?'\n      ).bind(id).first();\n    } catch {\n      // videos table may not exist \u2014 fallback empty\n    }\n    const videoCount = videoStats?.count || 0;\n    const totalDuration = videoStats?.total_duration || 0;\n    const avgDuration = videoCount > 0 ? Math.round(totalDuration / videoCount * 10) / 10 : 0;\n\n    return c.json({\n      course: {\n        ...(course as any),\n        duration: avgDuration,\n        total_videos: videoCount,\n        total_video_duration: totalDuration,\n      },\n      instructors,\n      learningPoints,\n      subjects,\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /courses/:id/curriculum \u2014 Get full curriculum structure for a course\nstudentApiRoutes.get('/courses/:id/curriculum', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const id = c.req.param('id');\n\n    // Verify course exists\n    const course = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT id FROM courses WHERE id = ? AND is_published = 1'\n    ).bind(id).first();\n\n    if (!course) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Course not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    // Fetch subjects for this course via course_subjects join table\n    let subjects: unknown[] = [];\n    try {\n      const subResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        'SELECT s.* FROM subjects s JOIN course_subjects cs ON s.id = cs.subject_id WHERE cs.course_id = ? OR id = ? LIMIT 1'\n      ).bind(key, key).first<{ course_id: string; is_preview: number }>();\n\n      if (video) {\n        const enrollment = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n          'SELECT id FROM enrollments WHERE user_id = ? AND course_id = ?'\n        ).bind(auth.userId, video.course_id).first();\n\n        if (!enrollment && !video.is_preview) {\n          return c.json({ error: 'Not enrolled in this course' }, 403);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    const url = getPublicUrl(c.env, bucket, key);\n\n    return c.json({ url });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n
