Create tables\n  for (const sql of createTables) {\n    results.push(await execIgnore(c.env.DB, sql));\n  }\n\n  // 2. Alter tables (add missing columns)\n  for (const sql of alterStatements) {\n    results.push(await execIgnore(c.env.DB, sql));\n  }\n\n  // 3. Create indexes\n  for (const sql of createIndexes) {\n    results.push(await execIgnore(c.env.DB, sql));\n  }\n\n  // 4. Seed data\n  for (const sql of seedStatements) {\n    results.push(await execIgnore(c.env.DB, sql));\n  }\n\n  // 5. AND is_active = 1'\n      ).bind(courseId).all();\n\n      if ((existingPackages.results as any[]).length > 0) {\n        results.push({ sql: `Skipping auto-package for course ${courseId} (already has ${existingPackages.results.length} packages)`, ok: true });\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      // Single package (1 user \u2014 original price)\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n        INSERT INTO results.push({ sql: `Auto-package for course ${courseId}`, ok: true });\n    }\n  } catch (autoPkgErr) {\n    results.push({ sql: 'Auto-package creation', ok: false, error: String(autoPkgErr) });\n  }\n\n  // Log the migration\n  await logAudit(c.env, user.id, 'RUN_MIGRATION', 'system', undefined, {\n    totalStatements: results.length,\n    failed: results.filter(r => !r.ok).length,\n  });\n\n  const failed = results.filter(r => !r.ok);\n  const ignored = results.filter(r => r.error?.startsWith('ignored:'));\n\n  return c.json({\n    success: failed.length === 0,\n    message: `Migration complete: ${results.length} statements, ${ignored.length} ignored (already exists), ${failed.length} failed`,\n    totalStatements: results.length,\n    ignoredCount: ignored.length,\n    failedCount: failed.length,\n    failedStatements: failed.map(r => ({ sql: r.sql, error: r.error })),\n    results: results.map(r => ({ sql: r.sql, ok: r.ok, error: r.error })),\n  });\n});\n\n// GET / \u2014 Check current schema status\nmigrateRoutes.get('/', adminAuthMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const tables = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      \"SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' ORDER BY name\"\n    ).all();\n\n    const tableInfo: Record<string, string[]> = {};\n    for (const table of tables.results) {\n      const tableName = table.name as string;\n      if (tableName.startsWith('_cf_')) continue; // skip Cloudflare internal tables\n      try {\n        const cols = await c.env.DB.prepare(`PRAGMA table_info('${tableName}')`).all();\n        tableInfo[tableName] = cols.results.map((c: any) => `${c.name} (${c.type})`);\n      } catch {\n        tableInfo[tableName] = ['ERROR reading columns'];\n      }\n    }\n\n    return c.json({\n      tableCount: tables.results.length,\n      tables: tableInfo,\n    });\n  } catch (e: any) {\n    return c.json({ error: e.message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\nexport default migrateRoutes;\n", "/**\n * Watch History routes \u2014 Student-facing\n * GET  /api/watch-history       \u2014 List watch history for authenticated student\n * POST /api/watch-history       \u2014 Upsert a watch history entry\n * DELETE /api/watch-history     \u2014 Clear all watch history for student\n * DELETE /api/watch-history/:id \u2014 Delete a single history entry\n *\n * Uses the student_activity D1 table to persist watch events.\n */\n\nimport { Hono } from 'hono';\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport type { StudentAuthVariables } from '../lib/student-auth-middleware';\nimport { studentAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/student-auth-middleware';\nimport { generateId, getErrorMessage } from '../lib/utils';\n\nconst watchHistoryRoutes = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: StudentAuthVariables }>();\n\n// Apply student auth middleware to all routes\nwatchHistoryRoutes.use('*', studentAuthMiddleware);\n\n// GET / \u2014 List watch history for current student\nwatchHistoryRoutes.get('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const userId = c.get('studentId');\n    const limit = Math.min(parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '50'), 200);\n    const offset = parseInt(c.req.query('offset') || '0');\n\n    // Fetch watch history from student_activity table, joined with video/course info\n    const { results } = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT\n        sa.id,\n        sa.resource_id AS video_id,\n        sa.title AS video_title,\n        sa.metadata,\n        sa.created_at AS watched_at,\n        v.course_id,\n        v.duration AS video_duration,\n        v.thumbnail_url AS video_thumbnail,\n        c.title AS course_name,\n        c.thumbnail_url AS course_thumbnail\n      FROM student_activity sa\n      LEFT JOIN videos v ON v.id = sa.resource_id\n      LEFT JOIN courses c ON c.id = v.course_id\n      WHERE sa.user_id = ? AND sa.activity_type = 'watch'\n      ORDER BY sa.created_at DESC\n      LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`\n    )\n      .bind(userId, limit, offset)\n      .all();\n\n    // Get total count\n    const countResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM student_activity WHERE user_id = ? AND activity_type = 'watch'`\n    )\n      .bind(userId)\n      .first<{ total: number }>();\n\n    // Parse metadata JSON for each item\n    const history = results.map((row: any) => {\n      let metadata: Record<string, any> = {};\n      try {\n        metadata = row.metadata ? JSON.parse(row.metadata) : {};\n      } catch {}\n      return {\n        id: row.id,\n        videoId: row.video_id,\n        videoTitle: row.video_title || '',\n        courseId: row.course_id || '',\n        courseName: row.course_name || '',\n        watchedAt: row.watched_at,\n        progress: metadata.progress || 0,\n        lastPosition: metadata.lastPosition || 0,\n        duration: row.video_duration || metadata.duration || 0,\n        videoThumbnail: row.video_thumbnail || '',\n        courseThumbnail: row.course_thumbnail || '',\n      };\n    });\n\n    return c.json({\n      history,\n      total: countResult?.total || 0,\n      limit,\n      offset,\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    console.error('Watch history GET error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST / \u2014 Upsert a watch history entry\nwatchHistoryRoutes.post('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const userId = c.get('studentId');\n    const body = await c.req.json<{\n      videoId: string;\n      videoTitle?: string;\n      courseId?: string;\n      progress?: number;\n      lastPosition?: number;\n      duration?: number;\n    }>();\n\n    if (!body.videoId) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'videoId is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const id = generateId();\n    const metadata = JSON.stringify({\n      progress: body.progress || 0,\n      lastPosition: body.lastPosition || 0,\n      duration: body.duration || 0,\n      courseId: body.courseId || '',\n    });\n\n    // Check if an entry already exists for this user + video\n    const existing = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `SELECT id FROM student_activity WHERE user_id = ? AND activity_type = 'watch' AND resource_id = ?`\n    )\n      .bind(userId, body.videoId)\n      .first<{ id: string }>();\n\n    if (existing) {\n      // Update existing entry \u2014 bump timestamp to top of history\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        `UPDATE student_activity\n         SET title = ?, metadata = ?, created_at = datetime('now')\n         WHERE id = ?`\n      )\n        .bind(body.videoTitle || '', metadata, existing.id)\n        .run();\n\n      return c.json({\n        success: true,\n        id: existing.id,\n        action: 'updated',\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Insert new entry\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `INSERT INTO student_activity (id, user_id, activity_type, resource_type, resource_id, title, description, metadata, created_at)\n       VALUES (?, ?, 'watch', 'video', ?, ?, '', ?, datetime('now'))`\n    )\n      .bind(id, userId, body.videoId, body.videoTitle || '', metadata)\n      .run();\n\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      id,\n      action: 'created',\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    console.error('Watch history POST error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// DELETE / \u2014 Clear all watch history for current student\nwatchHistoryRoutes.delete('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const userId = c.get('studentId');\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `DELETE FROM student_activity WHERE user_id = ? AND activity_type = 'watch'`\n    )\n      .bind(userId)\n      .run();\n\n    return c.json({\n      success: true,\n      deleted: result.meta?.changes || 0,\n    });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    console.error('Watch history DELETE all error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// DELETE /:id \u2014 Delete a single watch history entry\nwatchHistoryRoutes.delete('/:id', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const userId = c.get('studentId');\n    const entryId = c.req.param('id');\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      `DELETE FROM student_activity WHERE id = ? AND user_id = ? AND activity_type = 'watch'`\n    )\n      .bind(entryId, userId)\n      .run();\n\n    if (!result.meta?.changes) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'History entry not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    return c.json({ success: true });\n  } catch (error) {\n    const message = getErrorMessage(error);\n    console.error('Watch history DELETE single error:', error);\n    return c.json({ error: message }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\nexport default watchHistoryRoutes;\n", "/**\n * About page routes \u2014 Public + Admin CRUD\n * - GET /api/about \u2014 Public: all about page content\n * - GET /admin/about \u2014 Admin: get all about content\n * - PUT /admin/about/content \u2014 Admin: update about text, mission, contact\n * - CRUD /admin/about/stats \u2014 Admin: manage stats\n * - CRUD /admin/about/team \u2014 Admin: manage team members\n * - CRUD /admin/about/faq \u2014 Admin: manage FAQ items\n */\n\nimport { Hono } from 'hono';\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport type { AuthVariables } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { adminAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { logAudit } from '../lib/audit';\nimport { getErrorMessage } from '../lib/utils';\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Default about content (fallback) \u2500\u2500\u2500\nconst DEFAULT_ABOUT_CONTENT = {\n  aboutText: \"DAKKHO is Bangladesh's premier online learning platform built exclusively for polytechnic students. {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Ticket not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const messages = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_messages WHERE ticket_id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n        ).bind(token).first<{ user_id: string; email: string; name: string }>();\n        if (session) {\n          senderName = session.name || session.email;\n        }\n      } catch {}\n    }\n\n    if (contentType.includes('multipart/form-data')) {\n      const formData = await c.req.formData();\n      message = (formData.get('message') as string) || '';\n      senderName = senderName || (formData.get('name') as string) || '';\n      senderType = (formData.get('senderType') as string) || 'user';\n\n      const files = formData.getAll('files') as unknown as File[];\n      for (const file of files) {\n        if (!file || file.size === 0) continue;\n        if (file.size > 10 * 1024 * 1024) continue;\n        const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();\n        const key = `support/${ticketId}/${Date.now()}-${file.name}`;\n        await uploadFile(c.env.R2_SUPPORT_ATTACHMENTS, key, arrayBuffer, file.type);\n        attachmentUrls.push(key);\n      }\n    } else {\n      const body = await c.req.json();\n      message = body.message || '';\n      senderName = senderName || body.name || '';\n      senderType = body.senderType || 'user';\n      attachmentUrls = body.attachmentUrls || [];\n    }\n\n    if (!message.trim()) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Message is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO support_messages (ticket_id, sender_type, sender_name, message, attachments, source)\n      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'app')\n    `).bind(ticketId, senderType, senderName, message, JSON.stringify(attachmentUrls)).run();\n\n    // Update ticket updated_at and reopen if was resolved\n    const newStatus = ticket.status === 'resolved' ? 'open' : ticket.status;\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      \"UPDATE support_tickets SET updated_at = datetime('now'), status = ? WHERE ticket_id = ?\"\n    ).bind(newStatus, ticketId).run();\n\n    // If user is replying, notify admin via Telegram\n    if (senderType === 'user') {\n      const { botToken, chatIds } = await getTelegramConfig(c.env);\n      for (const chatId of chatIds) {\n        await sendTelegramMessage(botToken, chatId,\n          `\uD83D\uDCAC <b>User Reply on ${ticketId}</b>\\n\\n` +\n          `\uD83D\uDC64 ${senderName}\\n` +\n          `\uD83D\uDCAC <i>${message.substring(0, 500)}${message.length > 500 ? '...' : ''}</i>\\n\\n` +\n          `Reply: /reply ${ticketId} Your message here`\n        );\n      }\n    }\n\n    return c.json({ success: true });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /attachment-url \u2014 Get a presigned/public URL for an attachment\nsupportPublicRoutes.get('/attachment-url', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const key = c.req.query('key');\n    if (!key) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'key is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    // Serve the file from R2 via our upload route\n    const file = await c.env.R2_SUPPORT_ATTACHMENTS.get(key);\n    if (!file) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'File not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const headers = new Headers();\n    if (file.httpMetadata?.contentType) {\n      headers.set('Content-Type', file.httpMetadata.contentType);\n    }\n    headers.set('Cache-Control', 'public, max-age=86400');\n    headers.set('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');\n\n    return new Response(file.body, { headers });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// ADMIN ROUTES (mounted on /admin/support)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nconst supportAdminRoutes = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env; Variables: AuthVariables }>();\nsupportAdminRoutes.use('*', adminAuthMiddleware);\n\n// GET /tickets \u2014 List all tickets (filterable)\nsupportAdminRoutes.get('/tickets', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const status = c.req.query('status') || 'all';\n    const priority = c.req.query('priority') || 'all';\n    const category = c.req.query('category') || 'all';\n    const search = c.req.query('search') || '';\n    const page = parseInt(c.req.query('page') || '1');\n    const limit = parseInt(c.req.query('limit') || '20');\n    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;\n\n    let query = 'SELECT * FROM support_tickets';\n    let countQuery = 'SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM support_tickets';\n    const conditions: string[] = [];\n    const params: unknown[] = [];\n\n    if (status !== 'all') {\n      conditions.push('status = ?');\n      params.push(status);\n    }\n    if (priority !== 'all') {\n      conditions.push('priority = ?');\n      params.push(priority);\n    }\n    if (category !== 'all') {\n      conditions.push('category = ?');\n      params.push(category);\n    }\n    if (search) {\n      conditions.push('(subject LIKE ? OR ticket_id LIKE ? OR email LIKE ? OR name LIKE ?)');\n      const searchParam = `%${search}%`;\n      params.push(searchParam, searchParam, searchParam, searchParam);\n    }\n\n    if (conditions.length > 0) {\n      const whereClause = ' WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ');\n      query += whereClause;\n      countQuery += whereClause;\n    }\n\n    query += ' ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?';\n\n    const countResult = await c.env.DB.prepare(countQuery).bind(...params).first();\n    const total = (countResult as any)?.total || 0;\n\n    const result = await c.env.DB.prepare(query).bind(...params, limit, offset).all();\n\n    return c.json({ tickets: result.results, total, page, limit });\n  } catch (error) {\n    return c.json({ error: getErrorMessage(error) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /tickets/:ticketId \u2014 Get ticket detail + messages\nsupportAdminRoutes.get('/tickets/:ticketId', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const ticketId = c.req.param('ticketId');\n\n    const ticket = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_tickets WHERE ticket_id = ?'\n    ).bind(ticketId).first();\n\n    if (!ticket) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Ticket not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const messages = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_messages WHERE ticket_id = ? // 10MB max\n        const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();\n        const key = `support/${ticketId}/${Date.now()}-${file.name}`;\n        await uploadFile(c.env.R2_SUPPORT_ATTACHMENTS, key, arrayBuffer, file.type);\n        attachmentUrls.push(key);\n      }\n    } else {\n      const body = await c.req.json();\n      message = body.message || '';\n      attachmentUrls = body.attachmentUrls || [];\n    }\n\n    if (!message.trim() && attachmentUrls.length === 0) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Message or attachment is required' }, 400);\n    }\n\n    const ticket = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT * FROM support_tickets WHERE ticket_id = ?'\n    ).bind(ticketId).first<{ status: string; user_id: string | null; email: string; ticket_id: string }>();\n\n    if (!ticket) {\n      return c.json({ error: 'Ticket not found' }, 404);\n    }\n\n    const user = c.get('user');\n\n    // Save reply message\n    await c.env.DB.prepare(`\n      INSERT INTO support_messages (ticket_id, sender_type, sender_name, message, attachments, source)\n      VALUES (?, 'admin', ?, ?, ?, 'admin')\n    `).bind(ticketId, user.name || 'Admin', message, JSON.stringify(attachmentUrls)).run();\n\n    // Update ticket status to in_progress if it was open\n    if (ticket.status === 'open') {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        \"UPDATE support_tickets SET status = 'in_progress', updated_at = datetime('now') WHERE ticket_id = ?\"\n      ).bind(ticketId).run();\n    } else {\n      await c.env.DB.prepare(\n        \"UPDATE support_tickets SET updated_at = datetime('now') WHERE ticket_id = ?\"\n      ).bind(ticketId).run();\n    }\n\n    // Notify user via push\n    if (ticket.user_id) {\n      await notifyTicketReply(c.env, ticket.user_id, ticketId, 'admin', message);\n      // Save notification for tray\n      const timestamp = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);\n      const notifUrl = `https://dakkho-student.pages.dev/help/contact-support/${ticketId}`;\n      await saveNotification(c.env, ticket.user_id, 'New Support Reply', message.substring(0, 200), notifUrl, 'info', 'support');\n    }\n\n    // Notify via Telegram about admin reply\n    const { botToken, chatIds } = await getTelegramConfig(c.env);\n    for (const chatId of chatIds) {\n      await sendTelegramMessage(botToken, chatId,\n        `\u2705 <b>Admin Reply on ${ticketId}</b>\\n\\n` +\n        `\uD83D\uDC64 ${user.name || 'Admin'}\\n` +\n        `\uD83D\uDCAC <i>${message.substring(0, 500)}${message.length > 500 ? }, 500);\n  }\n});\n\n// GET /stats \u2014 Support statistics\nsupportAdminRoutes.get('/stats', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const open = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      \"SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM ).first();\n    const resolved = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      \"SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM support_tickets WHERE status = 'resolved'\"\n    ).first();\n    const closed = await \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// TELEGRAM WEBHOOK (mounted on /api/webhook/telegram)\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n\nconst telegramWebhookRoutes = new Hono<{ Bindings: Env }>();\n\ntelegramWebhookRoutes.post('/', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const body = await c.req.json();\n\n    // Verify the bot token from query param for security\n    const botToken = c.req.query('token');\n    const { botToken: configToken } = await getTelegramConfig(c.env);\n    if (!configToken || botToken !== configToken) {\n      console.error('Telegram webhook auth failed. Token mismatch or missing config.');\n      return c.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 401);\n    }\n\n    // Handle both message and callback_query\n    const message = body.message || (body.callback_query?.message);\n    const text = body.message?.text || '';\n    const fromName = body.message?.from?.first_name || body.callback_query?.from?.first_name || 'Admin';\n    const chatId = String((body.message?.chat?.id) || (body.callback_query?.message?.chat?.id) || '');\n\n    if (!text && !body.callback_query) {\n      return c.json({ ok: true });\n    }\n\n    const trimmedText = (text || '').trim();\n\n    // Handle commands\n    if (trimmedText === '/start') {\n      await sendTelegramMessage(configToken, chatId,\n        `\uD83D\uDC4B <b>Welcome to DAKKHO Support Bot!</b>\\n\\n` +\n        `Commands:\\n` +\n        `/tickets [status] \u2014 List tickets\\n` +\n        `/view TK-XXXXXX \u2014 View ticket\\n` +\n        `/reply TK-XXXXXX message \u2014 Reply to i < bytes.length; i++) {\n    binary += String.fromCharCode(bytes[i]!);\n  }\n  return btoa(binary)\n    .replace(/\\+/g, '-')\n    .replace(/\\//g, '_')\n    .replace(/=+$/, '');\n}\n\nfunction base64urlDecode(str: string): ArrayBuffer {\n  let base64 = str.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');\n  const pad = (4 - (base64.length % 4)) % 4;\n  if (pad > 0) base64 += '='.repeat(pad);\n  const binary = atob(base64);\n  const bytes = new Uint8Array(binary.length);\n  for (let i = 0; i < binary.length; i++) {\n    bytes[i] = binary.charCodeAt(i);\n  }\n  return bytes.buffer;\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// Crypto Primitives (HMAC, HKDF)\n// ================================================================\n\nasync function hmacSHA256(key: ArrayBuffer, data: ArrayBuffer): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {\n  const cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\n    'raw',\n    key,\n    { name: 'HMAC', hash: 'SHA-256' },\n    false,\n    ['sign'],\n  );\n  return crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', cryptoKey, data);\n}\n\n/** HKDF-Extract per RFC 5869: PRK = HMAC-Hash(salt, IKM) */\nasync function hkdfExtract(salt: ArrayBuffer, ikm: ArrayBuffer): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {\n  return hmacSHA256(salt, ikm);\n}\n\n/** HKDF-Expand per RFC 5869 */\nasync function hkdfExpand(prk: ArrayBuffer, info: ArrayBuffer, length: number): Promise<ArrayBuffer> {\n  const hashLen = 32; // SHA-256\n  const n = Math.ceil(length / hashLen);\n  const infoBytes = new Uint8Array(info);\n\n  let okm = new Uint8Array(0);\n  let t = new Uint8Array(0);\n\n  for (let i = 1; i <= n; i++) {\n    // T(i) = HMAC-Hash(PRK, T(i-1) || info || i)\n    const data = new Uint8Array(t.length + infoBytes.length + 1);\n    data.set(t, 0);\n    data.set(infoBytes, t.length);\n    data[t.length + infoBytes.length] = i;\n\n    t = new Uint8Array(await hmacSHA256(prk, data.buffer));\n\n    const newOkm = new Uint8Array(okm.length + t.length);\n    newOkm.set(okm, 0);\n    newOkm.set(t, okm.length);\n    okm = newOkm;\n  }\n\n  return okm.slice(0, length).buffer;\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// ASN.1 / DER Helpers (for ECDSA signature conversion)\n// ================================================================\n\n/**\n * Convert a DER-encoded ECDSA signature to the raw r||s format\n * required by JWT (JWS) for ES256.\n *\n * DER:  0x30 <len> 0x02 <rLen> <r> 0x02 <sLen> <s>\n * Raw:  <r: 32 bytes> <s: 32 bytes>\n */\nfunction derToRawSignature(derSig: ArrayBuffer): ArrayBuffer {\n  const der = new Uint8Array(derSig);\n  let idx = 2; // skip SEQUENCE tag (0x30) + 1-byte length\n\n  // --- r INTEGER ---\n  if (der[idx] !== 0x02) throw new Error('Invalid DER signature: missing r INTEGER tag');\n  idx++;\n  const rLen = der[idx++];\n  const rDer = der.slice(idx, idx + rLen);\n  idx += rLen;\n\n  // --- s INTEGER ---\n  if (der[idx] !== 0x02) throw new Error('Invalid DER signature: missing s INTEGER tag');\n  idx++;\n  const sLen = der[idx++];\n  const sDer = der.slice(idx, idx + sLen);\n\n  const r = derIntegerTo32Bytes(rDer);\n  const s = derIntegerTo32Bytes(sDer);\n\n  const raw = new Uint8Array(64);\n  raw.set(r, 0);\n  raw.set(s, 32);\n  return raw.buffer;\n}\n\n/**\n * DER encodes integers with minimal bytes and a leading 0x00 when\n * the high bit is set (to indicate positive sign).  This function\n * strips any DER sign-padding and left-pads the value to exactly\n * 32 bytes (the P-256 field size).\n */\nfunction derIntegerTo32Bytes(derInt: Uint8Array): Uint8Array {\n  let value: Uint8Array;\n\n  if (derInt.length > 1 && derInt[0] === 0x00) {\n    // Strip the DER sign-padding byte\n    value = derInt.slice(1);\n  } else {\n    value = derInt;\n  }\n\n  if (value.length > 32) {\n    throw new Error(`DER integer too long (${value.length} bytes); expected \u2264 32`);\n  }\n\n  const result = new Uint8Array(32);\n  result.set(value, 32 - value.length);\n  return result;\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// Buffer Utilities\n// ================================================================\n\nfunction concat(...arrays: Uint8Array[]): Uint8Array {\n  const total = arrays.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.length, 0);\n  const result = new Uint8Array(total);\n  let offset = 0;\n  for (const a of arrays) {\n    result.set(a, offset);\n    offset += a.length;\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n\nfunction uint16BE(value: number): Uint8Array {\n  return new Uint8Array([(value >> 8) & 0xff, value & 0xff]);\n}\n\nfunction uint32BE(value: number): Uint8Array {\n  return new Uint8Array([\n    (value >> 24) & 0xff,\n    (value >> 16) & 0xff,\n    (value >> 8) & 0xff,\n    value & 0xff,\n  ]);\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// VAPID JWT Generation (RFC 8292)\n// ================================================================\n\n/**\n * Build and sign a VAPID JWT token.\n *\n * Header:  {\"typ\":\"JWT\",\"alg\":\"ES256\"}\n * Payload: {\"aud\":\"<origin>\",\"exp\":<now+43200>,\"sub\":\"<subject>\"}\n *\n * The private key must be a base64url-encoded PKCS8 DER EC P-256 key.\n */\nasync function generateVapidJwt(\n  privateKey: string,\n  audience: string,\n  subject: string,\n): Promise<string> {\n  // JWT Header\n  const header = base64urlEncode(\n    new TextEncoder().encode(JSON.stringify({ typ: 'JWT', alg: 'ES256' })),\n  );\n\n  // JWT Payload \u2014 exp = now + 12 hours (43200 seconds)\n  const payload = base64urlEncode(\n    new TextEncoder().encode(\n      JSON.stringify({\n        aud: audience,\n        exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + 43200,\n        sub: subject,\n      }),\n    ),\n  );\n\n  const signingInput = `${header}.${payload}`;\n\n  // Import the PKCS8 private key for signing\n  const cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\n    'pkcs8',\n    base64urlDecode(privateKey),\n    { name: 'ECDSA', namedCurve: 'P-256' },\n    false,\n    ['sign'],\n  );\n\n  // Sign \u2014 crypto.subtle returns a DER-encoded signature\n  const derSignature = await crypto.subtle.sign(\n    { name: 'ECDSA', hash: 'SHA-256' },\n    cryptoKey,\n    new TextEncoder().encode(signingInput),\n  );\n\n  // Convert DER \u2192 raw r||s (64 bytes) for JWT\n  const rawSignature = derToRawSignature(derSignature);\n\n  return `${signingInput}.${base64urlEncode(rawSignature)}`;\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// RFC 8291 \u2014 Push Message Encryption\n// ================================================================\n\n/**\n * Encrypt a push message payload per RFC 8291 using aes128gcm.\n *\n * Steps:\n *  1. Generate ephemeral ECDH P-256 key pair\n *  2. IKM  = ECDH(ephemeral_priv, recipient_pub)\n *  3. PRK  = HKDF-Extract(salt=auth_key, IKM)\n *  4. CEK  = HKDF-Expand(PRK, key_info,  16)\n *  5. Nonce= HKDF-Expand(PRK, nonce_info, 12)\n *  6. Encrypt plaintext (= payload || 0x02) with AES-128-GCM\n *  7. Return: salt(16) || rs(4, 4096) || ephemeral_pub(65) || ciphertext\n *\n * @param payload  JSON string to encrypt\n * @param p256dh   Base64url-encoded uncompressed recipient public key (65 bytes)\n * @param auth     Base64url-encoded auth secret (16 bytes)\n */\nasync function encryptPayload(\n  payload: string,\n  p256dh: string,\n  auth: string,\n): Promise<Uint8Array> {\n  const recipientPub = new Uint8Array(base64urlDecode(p256dh));\n  const authKey = new Uint8Array(base64urlDecode(auth));\n\n  // 1. Generate ephemeral ECDH P-256 key pair\n  const ephemeral = (await crypto.subtle.generateKey(\n    { name: 'ECDH', namedCurve: 'P-256' },\n    true, // extractable \u2014 we need to export the public key\n    ['deriveBits'],\n  )) as CryptoKeyPair;\n\n  // Import the recipient's public key\n  const recipientCryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\n    'raw',\n    recipientPub,\n    { name: 'ECDH', namedCurve: 'P-256' },\n    false,\n    [],\n  );\n\n  // 2. Derive shared secret via ECDH\n  // Note: Cloudflare Workers types use \"$public\" instead of \"public\"\n  // because \"public\" is a reserved word in JavaScript.\n  const sharedSecret = await crypto.subtle.deriveBits(\n    { name: 'ECDH', $public: recipientCryptoKey },\n    ephemeral.privateKey,\n    256, // 32 bytes\n  );\n\n  // Export ephemeral public key as raw uncompressed (65 bytes)\n  const ephemeralPub = new Uint8Array(\n    (await crypto.subtle.exportKey('raw', ephemeral.publicKey)) as ArrayBuffer,\n  );\n\n  // Generate 16-byte random salt\n  const salt = crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(16));\n\n  // 3. PRK = HKDF-Extract(salt=auth_key, IKM=shared_secret)\n  const prk = await hkdfExtract(authKey.buffer as ArrayBuffer, sharedSecret);\n\n  // Build context per RFC 8291 \u00A73.1:\n  //   context = \"P-256\" || 0x00\n  //            || length(recipientPub) [2 bytes BE]\n  //            || recipientPub\n  //            || length(ephemeralPub)  [2 bytes BE]\n  //            || ephemeralPub\n  const context = concat(\n    new TextEncoder().encode('P-256'),\n    new Uint8Array([0x00]),\n    uint16BE(recipientPub.length),\n    recipientPub,\n    uint16BE(ephemeralPub.length),\n    ephemeralPub,\n  );\n\n  // 4. key_info = \"Content-Encoding: aes128gcm\" || 0x00 || context\n  const keyInfo = concat(\n    new TextEncoder().encode('Content-Encoding: aes128gcm'),\n    new Uint8Array([0x00]),\n    context,\n  );\n  const cek = await hkdfExpand(prk, keyInfo.buffer as ArrayBuffer, 16);\n\n  // 5. nonce_info = \"Content-Encoding: nonce\" || 0x00 || context\n  const nonceInfo = concat(\n    new TextEncoder().encode('Content-Encoding: nonce'),\n    new Uint8Array([0x00]),\n    context,\n  );\n  const nonce = await hkdfExpand(prk, nonceInfo.buffer as ArrayBuffer, 12);\n\n  // 6. Plaintext = payload || 0x02  (padding delimiter per RFC 8291 \u00A74)\n  const payloadBytes = new TextEncoder().encode(payload);\n  const plaintext = new Uint8Array(payloadBytes.length + 1);\n  plaintext.set(payloadBytes, 0);\n  plaintext[payloadBytes.length] = 0x02;\n\n  // AES-128-GCM encryption\n  const aesKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\n    'raw',\n    cek,\n    { name: 'AES-GCM' },\n    false,\n    ['encrypt'],\n  );\n\n  const ciphertext = await crypto.subtle.encrypt(\n    { name: 'AES-GCM', iv: nonce, tagLength: 128 },\n    aesKey,\n    plaintext,\n  );\n\n  // 7. Construct the encrypted content:\n  //    salt (16) || rs (4, big-endian 4096) || ephemeralPub (65) || ciphertext+tag\n  return concat(\n    salt,\n    uint32BE(4096),\n    ephemeralPub,\n    new Uint8Array(ciphertext),\n  );\n}\n\n// ================================================================\n// Public API\n// ================================================================\n\n/**\n * Generate a new VAPID key pair (run once during setup, not at runtime).\n *\n * Returns:\n *   publicKey  \u2014 base64url-encoded uncompressed raw EC P-256 public key (65 bytes)\n *   privateKey \u2014 base64url-encoded PKCS8 DER EC P-256 private key\n */\nexport async function generateVapidKeys(): Promise<{ publicKey: string; privateKey: string }> {\n  const keyPair = (await crypto.subtle.generateKey(\n    { name: 'ECDSA', namedCurve: 'P-256' },\n    true, // extractable\n    ['sign'],\n  )) as CryptoKeyPair;\n\n  const publicKey = base64urlEncode(\n    (await crypto.subtle.exportKey('raw', keyPair.publicKey)) as ArrayBuffer,\n  );\n  const privateKey = base64urlEncode(\n    (await crypto.subtle.exportKey('pkcs8', keyPair.privateKey)) as ArrayBuffer,\n  );\n\n  return { publicKey, privateKey };\n}\n\n/**\n * Derive the uncompressed public key from a PKCS8 DER private key.\n *\n * This parses the PKCS8 structure synchronously (no crypto.subtle needed).\n * The ECPrivateKey inside PKCS8 includes the public key under the\n * context-specific [1] EXPLICIT tag (0xA1), which contains a BIT STRING\n * with the uncompressed point (0x04 || x || y).\n *\n * @param privateKey  Base64url-encoded PKCS8 DER private key\n * @returns           Base64url-encoded uncompressed public key (65 bytes)\n */\nexport function getUncompressedPublicKey(privateKey: string): string {\n  const der = new Uint8Array(base64urlDecode(privateKey));\n\n  // Walk the DER looking for the [1] EXPLICIT tag (0xA1) that wraps the\n  // public-key BIT STRING.  For a standard Web Crypto PKCS8 export of an\n  // EC P-256 key the layout ends with:\n  //\n  //   A1 <len>        \u2014 [1] EXPLICIT\n  //     03 42         \u2014 BIT STRING, length 66\n  //       00          \u2014 0 unused bits\n  //       04          \u2014 uncompressed point marker\n  //       <x: 32B>    \u2014 x-coordinate\n  //       <y: 32B>    \u2014 y-coordinate\n  //\n  // Total suffix: 1 + 1 + 1 + 1 + 1 + 1 + 64 = 70 bytes\n  // The 0xA1 tag sits at der.length - 70 (with single-byte lengths).\n\n  for (let i = der.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (der[i] !== 0xA1) continue;\n\n    let idx = i + 2; // skip 0xA1 tag + 1-byte length\n\n    // BIT STRING tag (0x03)\n    if (der[idx] !== 0x03) continue;\n    idx += 2; // skip tag + 1-byte length\n\n    // Unused-bits byte must be 0x00\n    if (der[idx] !== 0x00) continue;\n    idx += 1;\n\n    // Uncompressed point marker\n    if (der[idx] !== 0x04) continue;\n\n    // Extract the full 65-byte uncompressed point (0x04 || x || y)\n    if (idx + 65 > der.length) continue;\n\n    return base64urlEncode(der.slice(idx, idx + 65));\n  }\n\n  throw new Error('Could not extract public key from PKCS8 DER \u2014 [1] EXPLICIT tag not found');\n}\n\n/**\n * Send a Web Push message to a Push Subscription endpoint.\n *\n * @param env          Environment with VAPID credentials\n * @param subscription Browser PushSubscription-like object\n * @param payload      JSON-serializable object to send\n * @param options      Optional TTL and urgency headers\n */\nexport async function sendWebPush(\n  env: {\n    VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY: string;\n    VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY: string;\n    VAPID_SUBJECT: string;\n  },\n  subscription: {\n    endpoint: string;\n    keys: { p256dh: string; auth: string };\n  },\n  payload: Record<string, unknown>,\n  options?: {\n    ttl?: number;\n    urgency?: 'very-low' | 'low' | 'normal' | 'high';\n  },\n): Promise<{ success: boolean; status: number; error?: string }> {\n  try {\n    // Audience = origin of the push endpoint (e.g. \"https://fcm.googleapis.com\")\n    const audience = new URL(subscription.endpoint).origin;\n\n    // Generate VAPID JWT\n    const jwt = await generateVapidJwt(env.VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY, audience, env.VAPID_SUBJECT);\n\n    // Encrypt payload per RFC 8291\n    const encrypted = await encryptPayload(\n      JSON.stringify(payload),\n      subscription.keys.p256dh,\n      subscription.keys.auth,\n    );\n\n    // POST to the push subscription endpoint\n    const response = await fetch(subscription.endpoint, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: {\n        Authorization: `vapid t=${jwt}, k=${env.VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY}`,\n        'Content-Encoding': 'aes128gcm',\n        'Content-Type': 'application/octet-stream',\n        TTL: String(options?.ttl ?? 2419200),\n        Urgency: options?.urgency ?? 'normal',\n      },\n      body: encrypted.buffer as ArrayBuffer,\n    });\n\n    return {\n      success: response.ok,\n      status: response.status,\n      ...(response.ok ? {} : { error: `Push service returned ${response.status}` }),\n    };\n  } catch (err) {\n    return {\n      success: false,\n      status: 0,\n      error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',\n    };\n  }\n}\n", "/**\n * Video Streaming & Processing Routes\n * \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n * - Tokenized HLS streaming for students\n * - Processing status updates from VPS transcoder\n * - Segment proxy with auth validation\n */\n\nimport { Hono } from 'hono';\nimport type { Env } from '../env';\nimport type { AuthVariables } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { adminAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/auth';\nimport { studentAuthMiddleware } from '../lib/student-auth-middleware';\nimport type { StudentAuthVariables } from '../lib/student-auth-middleware';\nimport { getErrorMessage } from '../lib/utils';\n\nconst videoStreamingRoutes = new Hono<{\n  Bindings: Env;\n  Variables: AuthVariables & StudentAuthVariables;\n}>();\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Token Generation Helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nfunction generateStreamToken(videoId: string, sessionId: string, expiry: number, secret: string): string {\n  // Simple HMAC-like token using Web Crypto\n  const data = `${videoId}:${sessionId}:${expiry}`;\n  // Use a simple encoding for now \u2014 in production, use proper HMAC\n  const encoded = btoa(JSON.stringify({ v: videoId, s: sessionId, e: expiry }));\n  return encoded;\n}\n\nfunction validateStreamToken(token: string, videoId: string): { valid: boolean; sessionId?: string; expiry?: number } {\n  try {\n    const decoded = JSON.parse(atob(token));\n    if (decoded.v !== videoId) return { valid: false };\n    if (decoded.e && Date.now() > decoded.e) return { valid: false };\n    return { valid: true, sessionId: decoded.s, expiry: decoded.e };\n  } catch {\n    return { valid: false };\n  }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Student Streaming Endpoints \u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n// POST /session/:videoId \u2014 Create streaming session\nvideoStreamingRoutes.post('/session/:videoId', studentAuthMiddleware, async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const videoId = c.req.param('videoId');\n    const userId = c.get('studentId') as string;\n\n    // Check enrollment\n    const video = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT course_id, is_preview, processing_status, hls_ready, available_qualities FROM videos WHERE id = ?'\n    ).bind(videoId).first<{ course_id: string; c.json({ authenticated: false }, 401);\n    }\n\n    const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n    // Try admin session\n    const adminSession = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT user_id, email, name, role, expires_at, is_active FROM admin_sessions WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    ).bind(token).first<{ user_id: string; email: string; name: string; role: string; expires_at: string; is_active: number }>();\n\n    if (adminSession && new Date(adminSession.expires_at) > new Date()) {\n      return c.json({\n        authenticated: true,\n        role: adminSession.role || 'admin',\n        user: { id: adminSession.user_id, email: adminSession.email, name: adminSession.name, role: adminSession.role || 'admin' },\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Try instructor session\n    const instructorSession = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT user_id, email, name, avatar_url, expires_at, is_active FROM instructor_sessions WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    ).bind(token).first<{ user_id: string; email: string; name: string; avatar_url: string | null; expires_at: string; is_active: number }>();\n\n    if (instructorSession && new Date(instructorSession.expires_at) > new Date()) {\n      return c.json({\n        authenticated: true,\n        role: 'instructor',\n        instructor: {\n          id: instructorSession.user_id,\n          email: instructorSession.email,\n          name: instructorSession.name,\n          avatar_url: instructorSession.avatar_url,\n        },\n        user: {\n          id: instructorSession.user_id,\n          email: instructorSession.email,\n          name: instructorSession.name,\n          role: 'instructor',\n          avatarUrl: instructorSession.avatar_url || '',\n        },\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Try student session\n    const studentSession = await c.env.DB.prepare(\n      'SELECT user_id, email, name, expires_at, is_active FROM student_sessions WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1'\n    ).bind(token).first<{ user_id: string; email: string; name: string; expires_at: string; is_active: number }>();\n\n    if (studentSession && new Date(studentSession.expires_at) > new Date()) {\n      return c.json({\n        authenticated: true,\n        role: 'student',\n        user: {\n          id: studentSession.user_id,\n          email: studentSession.email,\n          name: studentSession.name,\n          role: 'student',\n        },\n      });\n    }\n\n    return c.json({ authenticated: false }, 401);\n  } catch {\n    return c.json({ authenticated: false }, 401);\n  }\n});\n\n// POST /logout \u2014 Unified logout (auto-detects session type)\nunifiedAuthRoutes.post('/logout', async (c) => {\n  try {\n    const authHeader = c.req.header('Authorization');\n    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {\n      return c.json({ success: true });\n    }\n\n    const token = authHeader.substring(7);\n\n    // Try to invalidate in all session tables\n    try { await c.env.DB.prepare('UPDATE admin_sessions SET is_active = 0 WHERE id = ?').bind(token).run(); } catch {}\n    try { await c.env.DB.prepare('UPDATE instructor_sessions SET is_active = 0 WHERE id = ?').bind(token).run(); } catch {}\n    try { await c.env.DB.prepare('UPDATE student_sessions SET is_active = 0 WHERE id = ?').bind(token).run(); } catch {}\n\n    return c.json({ success: true });\n  } catch {\n    return c.json({ success: true });\n  }\n});\n\nexport default unifiedAuthRoutes;\n"],
